```
     0x4AFD [0x01] GOTO 0x4B35
     0x4B00 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 3*) GOTO 0x4B15
     0x4B08 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 403*
     0x4B0D [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[19] = 0*
     0x4B12 [0x01] GOTO 0x4B35
     0x4B15 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 4*) GOTO 0x4B25
     0x4B1D [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 454*
     0x4B22 [0x01] GOTO 0x4B35
     0x4B25 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[20] == 5*) GOTO 0x4B35
     0x4B2D [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[18] = 455*

     0x4B35 [0x1B] RETURN
```
